[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **double-free vulnerability**, which is a type of memory corruption bug [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere the same dynamically allocated memory is freed more than once. Double-free [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerabilities can lead to:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory corruption[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Potential exploitation for arbitrary code execution[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Program crashes and denial of service[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Error Flow Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**First Free Operation:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe memory is first freed during the cleanup phase in `static_destruct` function at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m95[0m[39m of `src/basic/static-destruct.h`, which is called from the fuzzer test [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` at line [0m[1;36m74[0m[39m of [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c`.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Second Free Operation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDouble-Free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe same memory is attempted to be freed again in the `parse_path_argument` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction at line [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m of `src/shared/parse-argument.c`, which is called from:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `systemctl_parse_argv` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m732[0m[39m in `src/systemctl/systemctl.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Which is in turn called from `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m58[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Memory Allocation:**[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe memory was originally allocated via `realloc` in the `path_extend_internal` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction at line [0m[1;36m585[0m[39m of `src/basic/path-util.c`, through the following call chain:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `path_make_absolute_cwd` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m92[0m[39m of `src/basic/path-util.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m72[0m[39m of `src/shared/parse-argument.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `systemctl_parse_argv` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m732[0m[39m of `src/systemctl/systemctl.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Timing**: The double-free occurs within the same thread [0m[1;39m([0m[39mT0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during a single [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest iteration, suggesting a logical error in memory ownership or cleanup [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Region**: The affected memory is a small [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-byte region, likely [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining a path string or related metadata.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Call Stack Pattern**: The issue involves path processing functionality, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically related to making paths absolute and parsing path arguments for [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystemctl.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Static Destructor Involvement**: The involvement of `static_destruct` suggests[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat there may be issues with cleanup of static or global resources, potentially [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating that memory is being tracked for automatic cleanup while also being [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanually freed.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a holistic understanding of this issue, the following components should [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe examined:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **`src/shared/parse-argument.c`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m and surrounding context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review the memory management logic in `parse_path_argument`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Understand ownership semantics of the path argument being freed[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **`src/basic/static-destruct.h`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m95[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Examine how static destructors are registered and executed[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Understand what resources are being tracked for automatic cleanup[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **`src/systemctl/systemctl.c`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m732[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review how `parse_path_argument` is called from `systemctl_parse_argv`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Check if there are any assumptions about memory ownership[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **`src/basic/path-util.c`**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review `path_extend_internal` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m585[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `path_make_absolute_cwd` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Understand the memory allocation strategy and ownership transfer[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **`src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m58[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m74[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review the fuzzer harness setup and teardown sequence[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Check for any initialization or cleanup code that might affect memory [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Memory Ownership Design**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Investigate whether there's a conflict between manual memory management and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mautomatic cleanup mechanisms[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Determine if the same pointer is being stored in multiple locations with [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdifferent cleanup responsibilities[0m                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I can identify the root [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the double-free vulnerability:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe double-free occurs due to a lifecycle mismatch between two memory management [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanisms:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Static Destructor Mechanism**: Global variables `arg_root` and `arg_image` are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregistered with `[0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[39marg_root, freep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[39marg_image, freep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in `src/systemctl/systemctl.c` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m136[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m137[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This registers them for automatic cleanup via `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Manual Memory Management**: The `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof `src/shared/parse-argument.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m explicitly frees the old value before assigning a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnew one using `[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg, p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Iteration Pattern**: The fuzzer at [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c` line [0m[1;36m74[0m[39m calls `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclean up global state between iterations, but **does not reset the freed pointers [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto NULL**.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### The Double-Free Sequence[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **First fuzzer iteration**: `arg_root` starts as NULL, gets allocated by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, then freed by `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m74[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **After cleanup**: `arg_root` becomes a dangling pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpointing to freed [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of NULL[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Second fuzzer iteration**: If `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called again with [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`arg_root` as a dangling pointer, line [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m's `[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg, p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` attempts to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfree the already-freed memory → **DOUBLE-FREE**[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Code Evidence[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFrom `src/basic/alloc-util.h:[0m[1;36m105[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m107[0m[39m`:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic inline void [0m[1;35mfreep[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid *p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid**[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `[0m[1;35mfreep[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` function used by `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` only frees the memory but **does[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot nullify the original global variable pointer**. This leaves `arg_root` and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`arg_image` as dangling pointers after cleanup.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must be applied to the fuzzer harness code at [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c`. After `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m74[0m[39m, we need to explicitly reset the freed global pointers to NULL to prevent [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free on subsequent iterations.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Detailed Fix Steps[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: After line [0m[1;36m74[0m[39m in `src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c`, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately reset the global pointers that were freed by `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m* Reset freed pointers to NULL to prevent double-free on next iteration *[0m[35m/[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marg_root = NULL;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marg_image = NULL;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Review if other global pointers registered with [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`STATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER` also need resetting. From `src/systemctl/systemctl.c` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m130[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m143[0m[39m:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `arg_types`, `arg_states`, `arg_properties` - use `strv_freep`, sets to NULL [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mautomatically[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `_arg_job_mode`, `arg_kill_whom`, `arg_reboot_argument`, `arg_host`, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`arg_boot_loader_entry`, `arg_drop_in` - use `unsetp`, sets to NULL automatically[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `arg_wall`, `arg_clean_what` - use `strv_freep`, sets to NULL automatically[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `arg_image_policy` - uses `image_policy_freep`, needs verification[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOnly `arg_root` and `arg_image` use `freep` which doesn't nullify the original [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer, so only these need explicit resetting.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m**: Verify that `arg_image_policy` doesn't need similar treatment by [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking if `image_policy_freep` nullifies the pointer.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: Only modifies the fuzzer harness, not the production code. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe production code's memory management design is correct for single-execution [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand-line tools.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: The `STATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER` mechanism and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` function remain unchanged. They work correctly in their [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended use case [0m[1;39m([0m[39msingle program execution[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fuzzer-Specific**: The issue only manifests in fuzzing scenarios where the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame process is reused for multiple iterations. Normal systemctl execution doesn't [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhave this problem.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Matches Existing Pattern**: The fuzzer already resets `optind` and [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`arg_transport` at lines [0m[1;36m55[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m56[0m[39m, acknowledging the need to reset global state [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbetween iterations. This fix extends that pattern to cover all globals that might [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause issues.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Safe for NULL**: `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is explicitly designed to handle NULL[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas documented at line [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m: [0m[32m"do not pass in uninitialized pointers"[0m[39m - but [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL counts as properly initialized[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: If other fuzzers use `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` similarly, they may [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhave the same issue.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: Review other fuzzers in the codebase, but this appears to be [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munique to the systemctl fuzzer based on the code analysis.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: If new global variables are added with [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, freep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, they'll need similar handling.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: Add a comment explaining why these resets are necessary, serving [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas documentation for future maintainers.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m**: If `arg_image_policy` also suffers from the same issue.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: Need to verify the implementation of `image_policy_freep` to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetermine if it nullifies the pointer. If not, add it to the reset list.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Approaches Considered and Rejected[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Modify `[0m[1;35mfreep[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to nullify the pointer**: Would require changing [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/basic/alloc-util.h` which could have widespread effects across the codebase. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe current behavior of `[0m[1;35mfreep[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` may be intentional for other use cases.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Remove `STATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER` for `arg_root` and `arg_image`**: Would [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause memory leaks in normal systemctl execution. These globals need automatic [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup at program exit.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Change `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to not free the old value**: Would break the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocumented API contract and could cause memory leaks in legitimate multi-call [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscenarios.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Use `unsetp` instead of `freep` in STATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER**: Would cause [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory leaks because the allocated memory wouldn't be freed, only the pointer would[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe nullified.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy correctly addresses the double-free by ensuring that global [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointers are in a clean, initialized state [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m between fuzzer iterations, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching their state at program startup. It preserves all existing functionality [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile making the fuzzer safe for repeated iterations in the same process.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
